**tasmād uśīnara-titikṣū dvau putrāv utpannau ||8|| uśīnarasyāpi śivi-nṛga-nara-kṛmi-varmākhyāḥ paṁ ca putrā babhūvuḥ ||9|| pṛṣadarbha-suvīra-kekaya-madrakāś catvāraḥ śibi-putrāḥ ||10|| titikṣor api ruśadrathaḥ putro’bhūt ||11|| tasyāpi hemaḥ, hemasyāpi sutapāḥ, sutapasaś ca baliḥ ||12|| yasya kṣetre dīrghatama-sāṅga-baṅga-kaliṅga-suhma-pauṇḍrākhyaṁ bāleyaṁ kṣatram ajanyata ||13|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **aṣṭādaśe'nujasyānovaṁśaḥ samanuvarṇitaḥ | prātilomyāt samutpatteryo'sau sūtatvāmāgataḥ | bale kṣetre bhāryāyāṁ jātatvād bāleyam ||13||



**tan-nāma-santati-saṁjñāś ca pañca-viṣayā babhūvuḥ ||14|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **tannāmeti—teṣāmaṅgādīnāṁ nāmāni yāsāṁ santatīnāṁ tāsāṁ saṁjñā yeṣāṁ te viṣayā deśā babhūvuḥ ||14||



**aṅgād anapānaḥ, tato divirathaḥ, tasmād dharmarathaḥ ||15|| **



**tataś citraratho romapāda-saṁjñaḥ ||16|| **



**yasya daśaratho mitraṁ jajñe ||17|| **



**yasyājaputro daśarathaḥ śāntāṁ nāma kānyāṁ anapatyasya duhitṛtve yuyoja ||18||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tataścitraratha iti—yasya putro romapādasaṁjño daśaratho jajñe, yasmai ajaputro daśarathaḥ svakanyāṁ duhitṛtve yuyoja dattavānity arthaḥ ||18||



**romapādāc caturaṅgaḥ, tasmāt pṛthulākṣaḥ ||19|| **



**tataś campo yaś campāṁ niveśayāmāsa ||20|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **campāṁ purīm ||20||



**campasya haryaṅgo nāmātmajo’bhūt ||21|| **



**haryaṅgād bhadrarathaḥ, bhadrarathād bṛhadrathaḥ, bṛhadrathād bṛhatkarmā, bṛhatkarmaṇaś ca bṛhadbhānuḥ, tasmāc ca bṛhanmanā, bṛhanmanaso jayadrathaḥ ||22|| **



**jayadratho brahma-kṣatrāntarāla-sambhūtyāṁ patnyāṁ vijayaṁ nāma putram ajījanat ||23|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **prātilomyena brahmakṣatrayorantarāle saṅkare sambhūtirjanma yasyāstasyāṁ sūtāyāmity arthaḥ | brāhmaṇyāṁ kṣatriyājjātaḥ sūtaḥ iti smṛteḥ, ato mātṛvadāvarṇasaṅkarā iti vacanād vijayaḥ sūta eva, ataśca karṇo'pi tadvaṁśyatvāt sūtatvena khyātaḥ ||23||



**vijayaś ca dhṛtiṁ putram avāpa ||24|| **



**tasyāpi dhṛtavrataḥ putro’bhūt ||25|| **



**dhṛtavratāt satyakarmā ||26|| **



**satyakarmaṇas tv atirathaḥ ||27|| **



**yo gaṅgāṅgato mañjūṣā-gataṁ pṛthāpaviddhaṁ karṇaṁ putram avāpa ||28|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **mañjūṣāgataṁ kāṣṭhapiñjarasthaṁ, pṛthayā kuntyā apaviddhaṁ kanyāvasthāyāṁ jātatvāt lajjayā parityaktaṁ karṇaṁ putramavāpa | 



mātāpitṛbhyāmutsṛṣṭa tayoranyatareṇa vā | 

yaṁ putra parigṛhaṇīyādapaviddhaḥ sa ucyate | iti smṛteḥ ||28|| 



**karṇād vṛṣasena ity etad-antā aṅga-vaṁśyāḥ ||29|| **



**ataś ca puru-vaṁśaṁ śrotum arhasi ||30||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **ityete aṅgā aṅgavaṁśyāḥ ||29-30|| 



iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ caturthe'ṁśe aṣṭādaśo'dhyāyaḥ ||



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe caturthe’ṁśe aṣṭādaśo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(4.19\)



## puru-vaṁśa-kathanam



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**puror janamejayaḥ, tasyāpi pracinvān, pracinvataḥ pravīraḥ, pravīrān manasy urmanasyoś cābhayadaḥ, tasyāpi sudyuḥ, sudyor bahugataḥ, tasyāpi saṁyātiḥ, saṁyāter ahaṁyātiḥ, tato raudrāśvaḥ ||1||**



**ṛteṣu-kakṣeṣu-sthaṇḍileṣu-kṛteṣu-jaleṣu-dharmeṣu-dhṛteṣu-sthaleṣu-sannateṣu-vaneṣu-nāmāno raudrāśvasya daśa putrā babhūvuḥ ||2|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **ūnaviṁśe kramaprāptaḥ purorvaṁśī nirūpyate | duṣmantād yatra bharato yannāmnā bhāratāstvime | ṛteyurity-ādiśabdāḥ prathamaikavacanāntānukaraṇānyetāni nāmāni yeṣāmātmajānāṁ te ityete raudrāśvāsyātmajā iti pāṭhaḥ sugamaḥ ||2||



**ṛteṣor antināraḥ putro’bhūt ||3|| sumatim apratirathaṁ dhruvaṁ cāpy antināraḥ putrān avāpa ||4|| apratirathasya kaṇvaḥ putro’bhūt ||5|| tasyāpi medhātithiḥ ||6|| yataḥ kāṇvāyanā dvijā babhūvuḥ ||7|| **



**apratirathasyāparaḥ putro’bhūd ailīnaḥ ||8|| ailīnasya duṣyantādyāś catvāraḥ putrā babhūvuḥ ||9|| duṣyantāc cakravartī bharato’bhūt ||10|| yan-nāma-hetur devaiḥ śloko gīyate ||11|| **



**mātā bhastrā pituḥ putro yena jātaḥ sa eva saḥ |**

**bharasva putraṁ duṣyanta māvamaṁsthāḥ śakuntalām ||12||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **duṣmanto mṛgayārtham araṇyaṁ gato viśvāmitrān menakāyāṁ jātāṁ śakuntalāṁ nāma kanyāṁ kaṇvāśrame dṛṣṭvā gāndharveṇa vivāhena saṅgamya garbham ādhāya sva-puraṁ gataḥ sarvaṁ visasmāra | yāṁ ca jāta-putraṁ kaṇva-prahitena śiṣyeṇānītāṁ smṛtvāpi lokāpavāda-bhayād asvīkurvantaṁ duṣmantaṁ prati devī-gīto'yaṁ ślokaṁ--māta iti | 



**bhastrā** carma-puṭakaṁ, tat-sthānīyā **mātā** vīryādhāra-mātraṁ, kintu **pitur** niṣektur eva **putraḥ** | kiṁ ca, **yena** pitrā **jāto** janitaḥ, **sa eva** putraḥ tad-aṁśa-bhūta-vīryopādānatvāt, ātmā vai jāyate putra iti vacanāc ca | ataḥ **putraṁ bharasva** bibhṛhi | **śakuntalāṁ** ca nirdoṣām **avamaṁsthā** iti bharata-nāma-niruktir api ||12||



**retādhāḥ putro nayati naradeva yama-kṣayāt |**

**tvaṁ cāsya dhātā garbhasya satyam āha śakuntalā ||13||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kiṁ ca rotadhāḥ retasā dhīyate vidhīyate retodhāḥ sarmaṇyasun | aurasaḥ pitro'yamakṣayāt narakāt tatrasthaṁ pitaram unnayati ūrddhva svarga nayati yadvā retodhāḥ retaḥ sektā taha putram unnayati | tataḥ kim, ata āha, tvaṁ tvasya bharatasya retodhāḥ retasektā iti satyamevāha, ato bharasvety arthaḥ | nāmāniruktirūpaikakāryaparatvāt śloka ityekavacanamaviruddham ||13||



**bharatasya patnī-traye nava putrā babhūvuḥ ||14|| **



**naite mamānurūpā ity abhihitās tan-mātaraḥ parityāga-bhayāt tat-putrān jaghnuḥ ||15|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **naite putrā mamānurūpā matsadṛśā bhavantīti bharatenoktasteṣāṁ mātaro'satputramātṛtvena veṇamātaramaṅga ivāsmān parityajya vanaṁ yāsyatīti parityāgabhayāt tān putrān jaghnuḥ ghātitavatyaḥ ||15||



**tato’sya vitathe putra-janmani putrārthino marutsomayājino dīrghatamasaḥ pārṣṇyapāstād bṛhaspati-vīryād utathya-patnyāṁ mamatāyāṁ samutpanno bharadvājākhyaḥ putro marudbhir dattaḥ ||16|| **



**tasyāpi nāma-nirvacana-ślokaḥ paṭhyate ||17|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **vitartha vyarthe sati | dīrghatamaseti, atreyaṁ kathā, bṛhaspategrajasya utathyasya mamatākhyāyāṁ bhāryāyā bṛhaspatiḥ kāmābhibhūto reto'sṛjit | tacca garbha praviśad garbhasthitena sthānasaṅkocabhayāt pāṣṇaryāghātenāpāstaṁ bahiḥpātitamapi amogavīryatayā bharadvājanāmā putro'bhavat | garbhasthaśca bṛhaspatinā śapto'ndho dīrghatamā nāmnābhavat | sa bharadvājo devairdattaḥ | tatra ca bharadvājanāmaniruktiparastanmātāpitrorvivādarupaḥ śloko devaiḥ paṭhitaḥ ||17||



**mūḍhe bhara dvājam imam bhara dvājaṁ bṛhaspate |**

**yātau yad uktvā pitarau bharadvājas tatas tv ayam ||18||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **mūḍhe\! mamate\! dvājaṁ dvābhyāmāvābhyāṁ jātimimaṁ putraṁ bhara puṣāṇa evaṁ bravuntaṁ bṛhaspati mamatāha—he bṛhaspate\! tvamevemaṁ dvājaṁ bhara iti rasamaparamuktvā parityajya pitarau mamatā-bṛhaspatī yat yasmāt yātau, tataḥ bharadvājaśabdokterbharadvāja-saṁjño'bhūd ity arthaḥ | yātau yadu dikhād iti pāṭhe vivadamānāvityadhyāhāryam ||18||



**bharadvājaḥ sa vitathe putra-janmani marudbhir dattaḥ, tato vitatha-saṁjñām avāpa ||19|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **bharadvājasyaiva bharataputrastavadaśāyāṁ vitathanāmno niruktamāha—bharadvājaśya iti | pitṛbhyāṁ gate sati marudabhirbhūto'pi marutstomayāgatuṣṭaistasya vitathe pitra janmani yato dattastato vitathasaṁjñāmavopatyarthaḥ ||19||



**vitathasyāpi manyuḥ putro’bhavat ||20|| **



**bṛhatkṣatra-mahāvīrya-naragargā abhavan manyu-putrāḥ ||21|| **



**narasya saṅkṛtiḥ, saṅkṛter guruprīti-rantidevau ||22|| **



**gargāc chiniḥ, tataś ca gārgyāḥ śainyāḥ kṣatropetā dvijātayo babhūvuḥ ||23|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **tatastābhyāṁ gāryāḥ śainyāśca gargavaṁśyatvāt śinivaṁśyatvācca samākhyātāḥ kṣatriyā eva kenacit kāraṇena brāhmaṇāśca babhūvuḥ ||23||



**mahāvīryāc ca durukṣayo nāma putro’bhavat ||24||**

****

**tasya trayyāruṇiḥ puṣkariṇyo kapiś ca putra-trayam abhūt ||25|| **



**tac ca putra-tritayam api paścād vipratām upajagāma ||26|| **



**bṛhatkṣatrasya suhotraḥ ||27|| **



**suhotrād dhastī ya idaṁ hastināpuram āvāsayāmāsa ||28||**



**ajamīḍha-dvijamīḍha-purumīḍhās trayo hastinas tanayāḥ ||29|| **



**ajamīḍhāt kaṇvaḥ ||30|| **



**kaṇvān medhātithiḥ ||31|| **



**yataḥ kāṇvāyanā dvijāḥ ||32|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **ajamīḍhasya kaṇvādirako vaṁśaḥ bṛhadiṣvādiraparo vaṁśaḥ, nīlādiraparaḥ kṣatrādiścāparaḥ ||32|| 



**ajamīḍhasyāsya putro bṛhadiṣuḥ ||33|| **



**bṛhadiṣor bṛhaddhanuḥ, bṛhaddhanuṣaś ca bṛhatkarmā, tataś ca jayadrathaḥ, tasmād api viśvajit ||34|| **



**tataś ca senajit ||35||**



**rucirāśva-kāśya-dṛḍhahanu-vatsahanu-saṁjñāḥ senajitaḥ putrāḥ ||36|| **



**rucirāśva-putraḥ pṛthusenaḥ pṛthusenāt pāraḥ ||37|| **



**pārān nīlaḥ ||38|| **



**tasyaikaśataṁ putrāṇāṁ ||39|| **



**teṣāṁ pradhānaḥ kāmpliyādhipatiḥ samaraḥ ||40|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **kāmpilyaṁ nagaraṁ tasyādhipatiḥ ||40|| 



**samarasyāpi pāra-supāra-sadaśvās trayaḥ putrāḥ ||41|| **



**supārāt pṛthuḥ pṛthoḥ sukṛtis tato vibhrājaḥ ||42|| **



**tasmāc cāṇuhaḥ ||43||**

****

**yaḥ śuka-duhitaraṁ kīrtiṁ nāmopayeme ||44|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **śukasya vyāputrasya duhitaraṁ, harivaṁśe tathaiva darśanāt |

tathoktam—



parāśarakulotpannaḥ śuko nāma mahāyaśāḥ | 

vyāsādaraṇyāṁ sambhūto vidhūmo'gnariva jvalan | 

sa tasyāṁ pitṛkanyāyāṁ pīvaryā janayiṣyati | 

kṛṣṇaṁ gauraprabhuṁ śambhuṁ tathā bhūriśrutaṁ jayam kanyāṁ kīttimatīṁ ṣaṣṭhī yoginīṁ yogamātaram | 

brahmadattasya jananīṁ mahiṣīmanuhasya ca || iti | 



vāyupurāṇe'pīdameva vacaḥ ||44||



**aṇuhād brahmadattaḥ ||45|| **



**tataś ca viṣvaksenaḥ, tasmād udaksenaḥ ||46|| **



**bhallābhas tasya cātmajaḥ ||47||**



**dvijamīḍhasya tu yavīnara-saṁjñaḥ putraḥ ||48|| **



**tasyāpi dhṛtimān, tasmāc ca satyadhṛtiḥ, tataś ca sannatimān ||49|| **



**sannatimataḥ kṛtaḥ putro’bhūt ||50|| **



**yaṁ hiraṇyanābho yogam adhyāpayāmāsa ||51|| **



**yaś caturviṁśatiṁ prācya-sāmagānāṁ saṁhitāś cakāra ||52|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **yaḥ kṛtaḥ caturviṁśati saṁhitāścakāra ||52|| 



**kṛtāc cogrāyudhaḥ ||53|| **



**yena prācuryeṇa nīpakṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ ||54|| **



**ugrāyudhāt kṣemyaḥ, kṣemyāt sudhīraḥ, tasmād ripuñjayaḥ, tasmāc ca bahuratha ity ete pauravāḥ ||55||**



**ajamīḍhasya nalinī nāma patnī, tasyāṁ nīla-saṁjñaḥ putro’bhavat ||56|| **



**tasmād api śāntiḥ, śānteḥ suśāntiḥ, suśānteḥ purañjayaḥ, tasmāc ca ṛkṣuḥ ||57|| **



**tataś ca haryaśvaḥ ||58|| **



**tasmān mudgala-sṛñjaya-bṛhadiṣu-yavīnara-kāmpilya-saṁjñāḥ, pañcānāṁ eva teṣāṁ viṣayāṇāṁ rakṣaṇāyālebhete mat-putrā iti pitrābhihitāḥ pāñcālāḥ ||59||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **nṛpāḥ kṣatriyāviśeṣasteṣāṁ kṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ | pañcānāṁ viṣacānāṁ madīyānāṁ deśānām ||59|| 



**mudgalāc ca maudgalyāḥ kṣatropetā dvijātayo babhūvuḥ ||60|| **



**mudgalād bṛhadaśvaḥ ||61|| **



**bṛhadaśvād divodāso’halyā ca mithunam abhūt ||62|| **



**śaradvataś cāhalyāyāṁ śatānando’bhavat ||63|| **



**śatānandāt satyadhṛtir dhanurvedāntago jajñe ||64|| **



**satyadhṛter varāpsarasam urvaśīṁ dṛṣṭvā retaskannaṁ śarastambe papāta ||65|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **śaradvato gautamāt | skannaṁ skhalitam | kṣatropetā dvijātaya iti kṣatriyā era santaḥ kenacit kāraṇena brāhmaṇā babhūvurity arthaḥ ||65|| 



**tac ca dvidhā-gatam apatya-dvayaṁ kumāraḥ kanyā cābhavat ||66|| **



**tau ca mṛgayām upayātaḥ śāntanur dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā jagrāha ||67|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṛpayeti nāma niruktyartham ||67|| 



**tataḥ kumāraḥ kṛpaḥ kanyā cāśvatthāmno jananī kṛpī droṇācāryasya patny abhavat ||68||**



**divodāsasya putro mitrāyuḥ ||69||**

****

**mitrāyoś cyavano nāma rājā ||70|| **



**cyavanāt sudāsaḥ, sudāsāt saudāsaḥ, saudāsāt sahadevaḥ, tasyāpi somakaḥ ||71|| **



**somakāj jantuḥ putra-śata-jyeṣṭho’bhavat ||72|| **



**teṣāṁ yavīyān pṛṣataḥ, pṛṣatād drupadaḥ, tasmāc ca dhṛṣṭādyumnaḥ, tato dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ||73||**



**ajamīḍhasyānya ṛkṣa-nāmā putro’bhavat ||74|| **



**tasya saṁvaraṇaḥ ||75|| **



**saṁvaraṇāt kuruḥ ||76|| **



**ya idaṁ dharma-kṣetraṁ kurukṣetraṁ cakāra ||77|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **kuruṇāṁ svenopalakṣitaṁ kṣetraṁ devaprasādāddharmakāraṇaṁ kṣetraṁ cakāra ||77|| 



**sudhanur jahnu-parīkṣit-pramukhāḥ kuroḥ putrā babhūvuḥ ||78|| **



**sudhanuṣaḥ putraḥ suhotraḥ, tasmāc cyavanaḥ, cyavanāt kṛtakaḥ ||79||**



**tataś coparicaro vasuḥ ||80|| **



**bṛhadratha-pratyagra-kuśāmbu-kucela-mātsya-pramukhā vasoḥ putrāḥ saptājāyanta ||81|| **



**bṛhadrathāt kuśāgraḥ, kuśāgrād vṛṣabhaḥ, vṛṣabhāt puṣpavān, tasmāt satyahitaḥ, tasmāt sudhanvā, tasya ca jatuḥ ||82|| **



**bṛhadrathāc cānyaḥ śakala-dvaya-janmā jarayā saṁhito jarāsandha-nāmā ||83|| **



**tasmāt sahadevaḥ, sahadevāt somapaḥ, tataś ca śrutiśravāḥ ||84|| **



**ity ete mayā māgadhā bhūpālāḥ kathitāḥ ||85||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **śakaladvayarūpaṁ janma yasya, jarayā rākṣasyā sandhito yojitaḥ ||19|| 



iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ caturthe'ṁśe ekonaviṁśo'dhyāyaḥ ||



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe caturthe’ṁśe ekonaviṁśo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(4.20\)



## kuru-vaṁśa-varṇanam



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**parīkṣito janamejaya-śrutasenograsena-bhīmasenāś catvāraḥ putrāḥ ||1|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **viṁśe tu kuruputrāṇāṁ vaṁśānāha parāśaraḥ yatra svapurasantāna dhṛtarāṣṭrādisantatiḥ || kuroḥ putrāṇāṁ madhye sudhanuṣo vaṁśa uktaḥ, idānīṁ kuruputrasyaiva parikṣito vaṁśa ucyate | paṁrikṣita iti ||1||



**jahnos tu suratho nāmātmajo babhūva ||2|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **kuruputrasyaiva jahnorvaṁśamāha—jahnor iti ||2|| 



**tasyāpi vidūrathaḥ ||3|| **



**tasmāt sārvabhaumaḥ, sārvabhaumāj jayatsenaḥ, tasmād ārādhitaḥ, tataś cāyutāyuḥ, ayutāyor akrodhanaḥ ||4|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **pūrvoktāt ajamīḍhaputrādṛkṣādanyaḥ ||4|| 



**tasmād devātithiḥ ||5|| **



**tataś ca ṛkṣo’nyo’bhavat ||6|| **



**ṛkṣād bhīmasenaḥ, tataś ca dilīpaḥ ||7|| **



**dilīpāt pratīpaḥ ||8||**



**tasyāpi devāpi-śāntanu-bāhlīka-saṁjñās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ ||9|| **



**devāpir bāla evāraṇyaṁ viveśa ||10|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **devāpervaṁśo nābhavadityāśayenāha—devāpir iti ||10||



**śāntanus tu mahīpālo’bhūt ||11|| **



**ayaṁ ca tasya ślokaḥ pṛthivyāṁ gīyate ||12|| **



**yaṁ yaṁ karābhyām spṛśati jīrṇaṁ yauvanam eti saḥ |**

**śāntiṁ cāpnoti yenāgryāṁ karmaṇā tena śāntanuḥ ||13|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **yaṁ yaṁ jantuṁ spṛśati, sa sa yauvanameti, śāntiñcāpnoti | etāvatā yauvanādirūpaṁ śaṁ kalyāṇaṁ tanotīti śāntanunāmanirukteti jñeyam ||13|| 



**tasya ca śāntano rāṣṭre dvādaśa-varṣāṇi devo na vavarṣa ||14|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **prasaṅgāt parivedanadoṣamāha—tasya ity-ādinā na vavarṣa bhagavān parjanya ityantena ||14||



**tataś cāśeṣa-rāṣṭra-vināśam avekṣyāsau rājā brāhmaṇān apṛcchat kasmād asmākaṁ rāṣṭre devo na varṣati ko mamāparādha iti ||15|| **



**tataś ca tam ūcur brāhmaṇāḥ ||16|| **



**agrajasya te hīyam avanis tvayā sambhujyate, ataḥ parivettā tvam ity uktaḥ sa rājā punas tān apṛcchat ||17|| **



**kiṁ mayātra vidheyam iti ||18|| **



**tatas te punar apy ūcuḥ ||19|| **



**yāvad devāpir na patanādibhir doṣair abhibhūyate tāvad etat tasyārhaṁ rājyam ||20|| **



**tad alam etena tu tasmai dīyatām ity ukte tasya mantri-pravareṇāśmasāriṇā tatrāraṇye tapasvino vedavāda-virodha-vaktāraḥ prayuktāḥ ||21|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **aśmasāriṇā aśmasārināmnā svayameva tapasviveśadhāriṇaḥ pravrājitāḥ ||21|| 



**tair asyāpy atiṛjumater mahīpati-putrasya buddhir veda-vāda-virodha-mārgānusāriṇya-kriyata ||22|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **atyṛjumate yathāśru tārthagrāhiṇaḥ ||22|| 



**rājā ca śāntanur dvija-vacanotpanna-paridevana-śokas tān brāhmaṇān agrataḥ kṛtvāgrajasya pradānāyāraṇyaṁ jagāma ||23||**



**tad-āśramam upagatāś ca tam avanatam avanī-pati-putraṁ devāpim upatasthuḥ ||24|| **



**te brāhmaṇā veda-vādānubandhīni vacāṁsi rājyam agrajena kartavyam ity arthavanti tam ūcuḥ ||25|| **



**asāv api devāpir vedavāda-virodha-yukti-dūṣitam aneka-prakāraṁ tān āha ||26|| **



**tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ śāntanum ūcuḥ ||27|| **



**āgaccha he rājann alam atrāti-nirbandhena praśānta evāsāv anāvṛṣṭi-doṣaḥ patito’yam anādi-kāla-mahita-veda-vacana-dūṣaṇoccāraṇāt ||28|| patite cāgraje naiva te parivetṛtvaṁ bhavatīty uktaḥ śāntanuḥ svapuram āgamya rājyam akarot ||29|| **



**veda-vāda-virodha-vacanoccāraṇa-dūṣite ca tasmin devāpau tiṣṭhaty api jyeṣṭha-bhrātary akhila-sasya-niṣpattaye vavarṣa bhagavān parjanyaḥ ||30||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **śāntanorvaśamativistareṇāgre vakṣyan prathamaṁ bāhlīkavaṁśamāha—bāhlīkasya iti ||30|| 



**bāhlīkāt somadattaḥ putro’bhūt ||31|| **



**somadattasyāpi bhūri-bhūriśravaḥ-śalya-saṁjñās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ ||32|| **



**śāntanor apy amara-nadyāṁ jāhnavyām udāra-kīrtir aśeṣa-śāstrārthavid bhīṣmaḥ putro’bhūt ||33|| **



**satyavatyāṁ ca citrāṅgada-vicitravīryau dvau putrāv utpādayāmāsa śāntanuḥ ||34|| **



**citrāṅgadas tu bāla eva citrāṅgadenaiva gandharveṇāhave nihataḥ ||35|| **



**vicitravīryo’pi kāśirāja-tanaye ambikāmbālike upayeme ||36|| **



**tad upabhogātikhedāc ca yakṣmaṇā gṛhītaḥ sa pañcatvam agamat ||37|| **



**satyavatī-niyogāc ca mat-putraḥ kṛṣṇa-dvaipāyano mātur vacanam anatikramaṇīyam iti kṛtvā vicitravīrya-kṣetre dhṛtarāṣṭra-pāṇḍū tat-prahita-bhujiṣyāyāṁ viduraṁ cotpādayāmāsa ||38||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **mamaparāśarasya putraḥ mataputraḥ mujiṣyāyāṁ dāsyām ||38||



**dhṛtarāṣṭro’pi gāndhāryāṁ duryodhana-duḥśāsana-pradhānaṁ putra-śatam utpādayāmāsa ||39|| **



**pāṇḍor apy araṇye mṛgayāyāṁ ṛṣi-śāpopahata-prajā-janana-sāmarthyasya dharma-vāyu-śukrair yudhiṣṭhira-bhīmasenārjunāḥ kuntyāṁ nakula-sahadevau cāśvibhyāṁ mādryāṁ pañca-putrāḥ samutpāditāḥ ||40|| **



**teṣāṁ ca draupadyāṁ pañcaiva putrā babhūvuḥ ||41|| **



**yudhiṣṭhirāt prativindhyaḥ, bhīmasenāc chrutasenaḥ, śrutakīrtir arjunāt, śrutānīko nakulāt, śrutakarmā sahadevāt ||42||**



**anye ca pāṇḍavānāṁ ātmajās tad yathā ||43|| **



**yaudheyī yudhiṣṭhirād devakaṁ putram avāpa ||44|| **



**hiḍimbā ghaṭotkacaṁ bhīmasenāt putraṁ lebhe ||45|| **



**kāśī ca bhīmasenād eva sarvagaṁ sutam avāpa ||46|| **



**sahadevāc ca vijayā suhotraṁ putram avāpa ||47|| **



**reṇumatyāṁ ca nakulo’pi niramitram ajījanat ||48|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **maṇipuraṁ nāma nagaraṁ tatpateḥ pujyāṁ putrikādharmeṇaṁ asyā yo jāyate putraḥ sa me putro bhavediti kanyādāturvābandhena ||48||



**arjunasyāpy alūpyāṁ nāga-kanyāyāṁ irāvān nāma putro’bhavat ||49|| **



**maṇipura-pati-putryāṁ putrikā-dharmeṇa babhruvāhanaṁ nāma putram arjuno’janayat ||50|| **



**subhadrāyāṁ cārbhakatve’pi yo’sāv atibala-parākramaḥ samastārātiratha-jetā so’bhimanyur ajāyata ||51|| **



**abhimanyor uttarāyāṁ parikṣīṇeṣu kuruṣv aśvatthāma-prayukta-brahmāstreṇa garbha eva bhasmīkṛto bhagavataḥ sakala-surāsura-vandita-caraṇa-yugalasyātmecchayā kāraṇa-mānuṣa-rūpa-dhāriṇo’nubhāvāt punar jīvitam avāpya parīkṣij jajñe ||52|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **parikṣīṇeṣu kuruṣviti bhagavatastadrakṣaṇe parikṣinnāmaniruktau ca hetuḥ | ātmecchāmātrakāraṇena mānuṣarūpaṁ dhartuṁ śīlaṁ yasya tasya, punarjīvitamavāpya parikṣit jajñe ||52||



**yo’yaṁ sāmpratam etad bhū-maṇḍalam akhaṇḍitā-yati-dharmeṇa pālayatīti ||53||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **sāmpratamityanena parikṣidrājyakāla eva parāśaramaitreyasaṁvāda iti gamyate | akhaṇḍitā āyatiḥ prabhāvo yatra tadyathā syāditi kriyāviśeṣaṇam | syāt prabhāve'pi āyatir ityamaraḥ | āyatiruttaraphalaṁ dhanādi sampat sā akhaṇḍitā yatra tad yathā syāditi vā ||53|| 



iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ caturthe'ṁśe viṁśo'dhyāyaḥ ||



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe caturthe’ṁśe viṁśo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(4.21\)



## bhāvi-nṛpa-vivaraṇam



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**ataḥ paraṁ bhaviṣyān ahaṁ bhūpālān kīrtayiṣyāmi ||1|| **



**yo’yaṁ sāmpratam avanīpatiḥ parīkṣit tasyāpi janamejaya-śrutasenograsena-bhīmasenāś catvāraḥ putrā bhaviṣyanti ||2|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **ekaviṁśe purovaṁśo bhaviṣya upavarṇyate | kṣemakaṁ prāpya yaḥ saṁsthāṁ kalāvupagamiṣyati | kuruputra-parikṣita ivāsyāpi janamejayādisaṁjñā eva catvāraḥ putrāḥ ||2|| 



**janamejayasyāpi śatānīko bhaviṣyati ||3|| **



**yo’sau yājñavalkyād vedam adhītya kṛpādastrāṇy avāpya viṣam aviṣaya-virakta-citta-vṛttiś ca āunakopadeśād ātma-jñāna-pravīṇaḥ paraṁ nirvāṇam avāpsyati ||4|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **tasya janamejayasya | ātmavijñānapravaṇastatparaḥ ||4||



**śatānīkād aśvamedha-datto bhavitā ||5|| **



**tasmād apy adhisīma-kṛṣṇaḥ ||6|| **



**adhisīma-kṛṣṇān nicaknuḥ ||7|| **



**yo gaṅgayāpahṛte hastināpure kauśāmbyāṁ nivatsyati ||8||**



**tasyāpy uṣṇaḥ putro bhavitā ||9|| **



**uṣṇād vicitrarathaḥ ||10|| **



**tataḥ śucirathaḥ ||11|| **



**tasmād vṛṣṇimāṁs tataḥ suṣeṇas tasyāpi sunīthaḥ sunīthān nṛpa-cakṣus tamsād api sukhāvalas tasya ca pāriplavas tataś casunayas tasyāpi medhāvī ||12|| **



**medhāvino ripuñjayas tato mṛdus tasmāc ca tigmas tasmād bṛhadratho bṛhadrathād vasudānaḥ ||13|| **



**tato’paraḥ śatānīkaḥ ||14||**

****

**śrīdharaḥ : **pūrvoktājanamejayaputrādaparaḥ śatānīkaḥ ||14|| 



**tasmāc codayana udayanād ahīnaras tataś ca daṇḍapāṇis tato niramitraḥ ||15||**

****

**tasmāc ca kṣemakaḥ ||16|| **



**atrāyaṁ ślokaḥ ||17||**



**brahma-kṣatrasya yo yonir vaṁśo rājarṣi-satkṛtaḥ |**

**kṣemakaṁ prāpya rājānaṁ saṁsthānaṁ prāpsyate kalau ||18||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **brahmaṇaḥ brāhmaṇasya kṣatrasya kṣatriyasya ca yoniḥ kāraṇaṁ kṣatriyair eva kaiścit tapo-viśeṣāt brāhmaṇyaṁ labdham iti pūrvaṁ tathoktatvāt | saṁsthāṁ samāptim ||18|| 



iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ caturthe'ṁśe ekāviṁśo'dhyāyaḥ ||



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe caturthe’ṁśe ekaviṁśo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(4.22\)



## bhāvi-kālinekṣvāku-vaṁśīya-nṛpāṇāṁ varṇanam



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**ataś cekṣvākavo bhaviṣyāḥ pārthivāḥ kathyante ||1||**

****

**bṛhadbalasya putro bṛhatkṣaṇaḥ ||2|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **somavaṁśa-bhaviṣyāṇāṁ rājñāmatra prasaṅgataḥ | dvāviṁśe sūryavaṁśyānāṁ bhaviṣyo vaṁśa ucyate | bṛhadbalasyeti-caturthe'dhyāye arjunatanayenābhimanyunā bhārate yuddhe kṣayamanīyatetyatra ca darsitastasyety arthaḥ ||2|| 



**tasmād urukṣayas tasmāc ca vatsavyūhas tataś ca prativyomas tasmād api divākaraḥ ||3|| **



**tasmāt sahadevaḥ sahadevād bṛhadaśvas tat-sūnur bhānurathas tasya ca pratītāśvastasyāpi supratīkas tataś ca marudevas tataḥ sunakṣatras tasmāt kinnaraḥ ||4|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **yatra tatra nāmnāṁ vailakṣaṇyaṁ dṛśyate, tatra kalpayugādibhedena vyavasthāpanīyam ||4|| 



iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ caturthāṁśe dvāviṁśadhyāyaḥ ||



**kinnarād antarikṣas tasmāt suparṇas tataś cāmitrajit ||5|| **



**tataś ca bṛhadrājas tasyāpi dharmī dharmiṇaḥ kṛtañjayaḥ ||6|| **



**kṛtañajyād raṇañjayaḥ ||7|| **



**raṇañjayāt sañjayas tasmāc chākyaḥ śākyāc chuddhodanas tasmād rāhulas tataḥ prasenajit ||8|| **



**tataś ca kṣudrakas tataś ca kuṇḍakas tasmād api surathaḥ ||9|| **



**tat-putraś ca sumitraḥ ||10|| **



**ity ete cekṣvākavo bṛhadbalānvayāḥ ||11|| **



**atrānuvaṁśa-ślokaḥ ||12||**



**ikṣvākūṇām ayaṁ vaṁśaḥ sumitrānto bhaviṣyati |**

**yatas taṁ prāpya rājānaṁ saṁsthāṁ prāpsyati vai kalau ||13||**



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe caturthe’ṁśe dvāviṁśo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(4.23\)



## magadha-vaṁśa-varṇanam



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**māgadhānāṁ bārhadrathānāṁ bhāvinām anukramaṁ kathayiṣyāmi ||1|| **



**atra hi vaṁśe mahā-bala-parākramā jarāsandha-pradhānā babhūvuḥ ||2||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **bārhadrarathānāṁ vaṁśe'pi bhaviṣyānavadan nṛpān | antyo ripuñjayo yatra tadante prāthavat kaliḥ | soma-sūryavaṁśayorbhaviṣyān nṛpānuktvā somavaṁśapallavabhūtānāṁ bārhadrathānāṁ bhaviṣyānāha—māgadhānām iti | tatra ca saṅgatyarthaṁ kīrttitānāmapi jarāsandhādīnāmanuvādaṁ kurvannayutāyuḥprabhṛtīn bhaviṣyānāha—atra hi ity-ādinā yāvatsamāpti ||1-2||



**jarāsandhasya putraḥ sahadevaḥ ||3|| **



**sahadevāt somāpis tasya śrutaśravās tasyāpy ayutāyus tataś ca niramitras tat-tanayaḥ sunetras tasmād api bṛhatkarmā ||4|| **



**tataś ca senajit tataś ca śrutañjayas tato vipras tasya ca putraḥ śuci-nāmā bhaviṣyati ||5|| **



**tasyāpi kṣemyas tataś ca suvrataḥ, suvratād dharmas tataḥ suśravāḥ ||6|| **



**tato dṛḍhasenaḥ ||7|| **



**tasmāt subalaḥ ||8|| **



**subalāt sunīto bhavitā ||9|| **



**tataḥ satyajit ||10|| **



**tasmād viśvajit ||11|| **



**tasyāpi ripuñjayaḥ ||12|| **



**ity ete bārhadrathā bhūpatayo varṣa-sahasram ekaṁ bhaviṣyanti ||13||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **bārhadrathā bṛhadarathavaṁśodbhavāḥ || bṛhadrathasya apatyāni pumāṁsaḥ bārhadrathāḥ teṣām | bṛhadrathaśabdapatyārtheṣṇapratyayaḥ | jarāsādhaḥ jarayā tadākhyayā rākṣasyā sandhā sandhānaṁ bhāgadrayasya melanaṁ yatra saḥ | vṛttametad varṇitamedādhastād | sa eva pradhānaṁ yeṣāṁ te jarāsandhapradhānāḥ | |13||



iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ caturthāṁśe trayoviṁśa'dhyāyaḥ ||





|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe caturthe’ṁśe trayoviṁśo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(4.24\)



## kali-kāla-sthita-nṛpāṇāṁ kali-dharmasya ca varṇanam, rāja-vaṁśa-varṇanopasaṁhāraś ca 



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**yo’yaṁ ripuñjayo nāma bārhadratho’ntyas tasyāmātyo suniko nāma bhaviṣyati ||1|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **caturviṁśe kalerdharmasaṁkhye kṣudrāstathā nṛpāḥ | bhūmergītāvaśikṣā ca vairāgyāya nirūpitāḥ | idānīntu tadvaṁśyāneva bhūbhujaḥ kālenālpabalapauruṣān malīmasān dasyuprāyāṁścāha—yo'yam ity-ādinā sarve pṛthivyāṁ bhūbhujo bhaviṣyanti ityantena ||1||



**sa cainaṁ svāminaṁ hatvā sva-putraṁ pradyotanāmānam abhiprekṣyati ||2|| **



**tasyāpi balāka-nāmā putro bhavitā ||3|| **



**tataś ca viśākhayūpaḥ ||4|| **



**tat-putro janakaḥ ||5|| **



**tasya ca nandivardhanaḥ ||6|| **



**tato nandī | ity ete’ṣṭatriṁśad-uttaram abda-śataṁ paṁ ca pradyotāḥ pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti ||7||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **pradyotāḥ pradyotanāmānaḥ atra ca rājñāṁ tadrājyānāṁ varṣasaṁkhyā āyurādyalpatva pradarśanaṁ vairāgyārtham ||7||



**tataś ca śiśunābhaḥ ||8|| **



**tat-putraḥ kākavarṇo bhavitā ||9|| **



**tasya ca putraḥ kṣemadharmā ||10|| **



**tasya ca putraḥ kṣemadharmā ||11|| **



**tasyāpi kṣataujāḥ ||12|| **



**tat-putro vidhisāraḥ ||13|| **



**tataś cājātaśatruḥ ||14|| **



**tasmād arbhakaḥ ||15|| **



**tasmāc codayanaḥ ||16|| **



**tasmād api nandivardhanaḥ ||17|| **



**tato mahānandī ||18|| **



**ity ete śaiśanābhā bhūpālās trīṇi varṣa-śatāni dviṣaṣṭy adhikāni bhaviṣyanti ||19||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **śaiśunāgāḥ śiśunāgāpatyāni ||19|| 



**mahānandinas tataḥ śudrā-garbho’tilubdho’tibalo mahāpadma-nābhā nandaḥ paraśurāma ivāparo’khila-kṣatrānta-kārī bhaviṣyati ||20|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **mahāpadma iti | koṭiśataguṇaṁ padmaṁ padmaśataguṇaṁ kharvaṁ taddaśaguṇaṁ punaḥ nikharvaṁ, taddaśaguṇaṁ mahāpadmamiheṣyate ityakto stāvatsaṁkhyakasya sainyasya dhanasya vā svāmī mahāpadmānandaḥ ||20||



**tataḥ prabhṛti śūdrā bhūpālā bhaviṣyanti ||21|| **



**sa caika-cchatrām anullaṅghita-śāsano mahāpadmaḥ pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyate ||22|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **ekameva chatraṁ yasyāṁ tām ||22|| 



**tasyāpy aṣṭau sutāḥ sumālyādyā bhavitāraḥ ||23|| **



**tasya mahāpadmasyānu pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti ||24|| **



**mahāpamda-putrāś caikaṁ varṣa-śatam avanī-patayo bhaviṣyanti ||25||**



**tataś ca nava caitān nadnān kauṭilyo brāhmaṇaḥ samuddhariṣyati ||26|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **nandān nandaṁ tataputrāṁśca kauṭilyaḥ kauṭilyapradhānaḥ vātsyāyana-viṣṇuguptādiparyāyaścāṇakyaḥ samuddhariṣyati unmūlayiṣyati ||26||



**teṣām abhāve mauryāḥ pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti ||27|| **



**kauṭilya eva candraguptam utpannaṁ rājye’bhiṣekṣyati ||28|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **candraguptaṁ nandasyaiva palyantarasya murāsaṁjñasya putraṁ mauryāṇāṁ prathamam ||28|| 



**tasyāpi putro bindusāro bhaviṣyati ||29|| **



**tasyāpy aśokavardhanas tataḥ suyaśās tataś ca daśarathaḥ, tataś ca saṁyutas tataḥ śāliśūkaḥ, tasmāt somaśarmā, tasyāpi somaśarmaṇaḥ śatadhanvā ||30|| **



**tasyāpi bṛhadratha-nāmā bhavitā ||31|| **



**evam ete mauryā daśa bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti abda-śataṁ sapta-triṁśad-uttaram ||32|| **



**teṣām ante pṛthivīṁ daśa śuṅgā bhokṣyanti ||33|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **śuṅgāḥ śuṅgasaṁjñāḥ ||33|| 



**puṣyamitraḥ senāpatiḥ svāminaṁ hatvā rājyaṁ kariṣyati tasyātmajo’gnimitraḥ ||34|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **tānevāha—puṣpamitra iti | puṣpamitraḥ śuṅgānāṁ prathamaḥ ||34|| 



**tasmāt sujyeṣṭhaḥ, tato vasumitraḥ, tasmād apy udaṅkaḥ, tato bhāgavataḥ ||35|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **anamitrādayo nava, evaṁ śuṅgā daśa ||35|| 



**tasmād devabhūtiḥ ||36|| **



**ity ete śuṅgā dvādaśottaraṁ varṣa-śataṁ pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti ||37||**



**tataḥ kaṇvān eṣā bhūr yāsyati ||38|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **kaṇvān kaṇvasaṁjñanṛpān bhūḥ yāsyati | tataḥ kaṇvāneṣā bhūryāsyati ||38||



**devabhūtiṁ tu śuṅga-rājānaṁ vyasaninaṁ tasyaivāmātyaḥ kāṇvo vasudeva-nāmā taṁ nihatya svayam avanīṁ bhokṣyati ||39|| **



**tasya putro bhūmitras tasyāpi nārāyaṇaḥ ||40|| **



**nārāyaṇātmajaḥ suśarmā ||41|| **



**ete kāṇvāyanāś catvāraḥ pañca-catvāriṁśad-varṣāṇi bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti ||42||**



**suśarmāṇaṁ tu kāṇvaṁ tad-bhṛtyo bali-pucchaka-nāmā hatvāndhra-jātīyo vasudhāṁ bhokṣyati ||43|| **



**tataś ca kṛṣṇa-nāmā tad-bhrātā pṛthivī-patir bhaviṣyati ||44|| **



**tasyāpi putraḥ śānta-karṇis tasyāpi pūrṇotsaṅgas tat-putraḥ śātakarṇis tasmāc ca lambodaras tasmāc ca pilakas tato meghasvātis tataḥ paṭumān ||45|| **



**tataś cāriṣṭakarmā tato hālāhalaḥ ||46|| **



**hālāhalāt palalakas tataḥ pulindasenas tataḥ sundaras tataḥ śātakarṇis tataḥ śivasvātis tataś ca gomati-putras tat-putro’limān ||47|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **kaṇvān kathaṁ bhūryāsyati tatrāha—devabhūtistv iti | śātakarṇītyupanāma ||47|| 



**tasyāpi śāntakarṇis tataḥ śivaśritas tataś ca śivaskandhas tasmād api yajñaśrīs tato dviyajñas tasmāc candraśrīḥ ||48|| **



**tasmāt pulomāciḥ ||49|| **



**evam ete triṁśac catvāry-abda-śatāni ṣaṭ-pañcā śadadhikāni pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti āndhra-bhṛtyāḥ ||50|| **



**saptābhīra-prabhṛtayo daśa gardabhilāś ca bhūbhujo bhaviṣyanti ||51|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **ete tu andhrabhṛtyāstriṁśadityanvayaḥ ||51||



**tataḥ ṣoḍaśa śakā bhūpatayo bhavitāraḥ ||52|| **



**tataś cāṣṭau yavanāś caturdaśa turuṣkārā muṇḍāś ca trayodaśa ekādaśa maunā ete vai pṛthivī-patayaḥ pṛthivīṁ daśa-varṣa-śatāni navaty-adhikāni bhokṣyanti ||53||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **ābhīrādyā maunāntā ekonāśītī rājāna ekonacaturdaśa-śatavarṣāṇi pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti ||53||



**tataś ca ekādaśa bhūpatayo’bda-śatāni trīṇi pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti ||54|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **tataśca paurāstrīṇyabdaśatāni bhokṣyanti | kvacit paurā ityatra punarmaunā iti pāṭhaḥ | tadā ābhīrādimadhyagaṇitānāmapi maunānāṁ vyatirekeṇa pūrvarājyavarṣasaṁkhyā, iyantu tataḥ pṛthageva maunānāṁ rājyavarṣaśatatrayasaṁkhyeti jñeyam ||54||



**teṣūtsanneṣu kaiṅkilā yavanā bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanty amūrdhābhiṣiktāḥ ||55|| **



**teṣāṁ apatyaṁ vindhya-śaktis tataḥ purañjayas tasmād rāmacandras tasmād dharmavarmā tato baṅgas tato’bhūn nandanas tataḥ sunandī tad-bhrātā nandiyaśāḥ śukraḥ pravīra ete varṣa-śataṁ ṣaṭ-varṣāṇi bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti ||56|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **kilakilānagarī tatra bhavāḥ kailikalāḥ, teṣāṁ mūrdhābhiṣikto mukhyaḥ | vindhyaśaktirmūdhābhiṣikta iti pāṭhe kṣatriyamukhya ity arthaḥ ||56||



**tatas tat-putrās trayodaśaite bāhlikāś ca trayaḥ ||57|| **



**tataḥ puṣpamitrāḥ paṭu-mitrās trayodaśaikalāś ca saptāndhāḥ ||58||**



**tataś ca kośalāyāṁ tu nava caiva bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti ||59|| **



**naiṣadhās tu ta eva ||60||**



**magadhāyāṁ tu viśvasphaṭika-saṁjño’nyān varṇān kariṣyati ||61|| **



**kaivarta-vaṭu-pulinda-brāhmaṇān rājye sthāpayiṣyati ||62|| **



**utsādyākhila-kṣatra-jātiṁ nava nāgāḥ padmāvatyāṁ nāma puryām anugaṅgā-prayāgaṁ gayāyāṁ ca māgadhā guptāś ca bhokṣyanti ||63|| **



**kośalāndhra-puṇḍra-tāmralipta-samudrataṭa-purīṁ ca devarakṣito rakṣitā ||64|| **



**kaliṅga-māhiṣa-mahendra-bhaumān guhā bhokṣyanti ||65|| **



**naiṣadha-naimiṣaka-kāla-kośakāñjana-padān maṇidhānyaka-vaṁśā bhokṣyanti ||66|| **



**trairājyamuṣika-janapadaān kanakāhvayo bhokṣyanti ||67|| **



**saurāṣṭrāvanti-śūdrābhīrān narmadāmarubhūviṣayāṁś ca vrātya-dvijābhīra-śūdrādyā bhokṣyanti ||68|| **



**sindhu-taṭa-dāvikorvī-candrabhāgā-kāśmīra-viṣayāṁś ca vrātya-mleccha-śūdrādayo bhokṣyanti ||69|| **



**ete ca tulyakālāḥ sarve pṛthivyāṁ bhūbhujo bhaviṣyanti ||70|| **



**alpa-prasādā bṛhatkopāḥ sarva-kālam anṛta-dharma-rucayaḥ strī-bāla-go-vadha-kartāraḥ parasvādāna-rucayo’lpa-sārās tamisra-prāyā uditāstamita-prāyā alpāyuṣo mahecchā hy alpa-dharmā lubdhāś ca bhaviṣyanti ||71|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṣatrajātiṁ kṣatrajāṁ saṅkarajātim ugrasūtādirūpām | ete tatastatputrā ityākabhyaśūdrā ityantāstulyakālāḥ khaṇḍamaṇḍalapatayo'lpaprasādatvā diviśiṣṭā bhūbhṛto bhaviṣyantītyanvayaḥ ||71|| 



**taiś ca vimiśrā janapadās tac-chīlānuvartino rājāśraya-śuṣmiṇo mlecchāś cāryāś ca viparyayeṇa vartamānāḥ prajāḥ kṣapayiṣyanti ||72||**

****

**śrīdharaḥ : **tulyaḥ kālaḥ yeṣāṁ te tulyakālāḥ samānakālā eka-kālīnā ity arthaḥ | uditāstamitaprāyāḥ uditā anantaramekha vinā vilambam astamitāḥ tatprāyāḥ utpannavinaṣṭaprāyā ity arthaḥ || rājāśrayeṇa śuṣmiṇo balinaḥ, na tu dharmeṇa | mlecchāścāryāśca viparyayeṇa malecchā madhye āryāścānte ityetadrūpeṇa ||72||



**tataś cānudinam alpālpa-hrāsa-vyavacchedād dharmārthayor jagataḥ saṅkṣayo bhaviṣyati ||73|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **jagati dharmasyānudiṁ hrāsādarthasya ca vyavacchedāt saṁkṣayo bhaviṣyati ||73|| 



**tataś cārtha evābhijana-hetuḥ ||74|| **



**balam evāśeṣa-dharma-hetuḥ ||75|| **



**abhirucir eva dāmpatya-sambandha-hetuḥ ||76|| **



**strītvam evopabhoga-hetuḥ ||77|| **



**anṛtam eva vyavahāra-jaya-hetuḥ ||78|| **



**unnatāmbutaiva pṛthivī-hetuḥ ||79|| **



**brahma-sūtram eva vipratva-hetuḥ ||80|| **



**ratna-dhātutaiva ślāghyatā-hetuḥ ||81|| **



**liṅga-dhāraṇam evāśrama-hetuḥ ||82|| **



**anyāya eva vṛtti-hetuḥ ||83|| **



**daurbalyam evāvṛtti-hetuḥ ||84|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **ratnatāmrabhāgitā ratnabhūtatāmrādīmattvameva pṛthivīheturuttama bhūmitve kāraṇaṁ, na tu puṇyatīrthādimattvam unnatāmbumatteti pāṭhe unnate giritaṭādāvambumattvam || vṛttiḥ jīvikā ||81-84||



**abhaya-pragalbhoccāraṇam eva pāṇḍitya-hetuḥ ||85|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhayagarbhoccāraṇaṁ bhayopadarśanapūrvakamuccāraṇam ||85|| 



**anāḍhyataiva sādhutva-hetuḥ ||86|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **dānameva dharmahetuḥ, na tu yāgādiḥ | āḍhyataira sādhutvahetuḥ ||86|| 



**snānam eva prasādhana-hetuḥ ||87|| **



**dānam eva dharma-hetuḥ ||88|| **



**svīkaraṇam eva vivāha-hetuḥ ||89|| **



**sadveṣa-dhāry eva pātram ||90|| **



**dūrāyatanodakam eva tīrtha-hetuḥ ||91|| **



**kapaṭa-veṣa-dhāraṇam eva mahattva-hetuḥ ||92|| **



**ity evam aneka-doṣottare tu bhū-maṇḍale sarva-varṇeṣv eva yo yo balavān sa sa bhūpatir bhaviṣyati ||93|| **



**evaṁ cātilubdhaka-rājāsahāḥ śailānāṁ antara-droṇīḥ prajāḥ saṁśrayiṣyanti ||94|| **



**madhu-śāka-mūla-phala-patra-puṣpādy-āhārāś ca bhaviṣyanti ||95|| **



**taru-valka-parṇa-cīra-prāvaraṇāś cātibahu-prajāḥ cītavātātapa-varṣa-sahāś ca bhaviṣyanti ||96|| **



**na ca kaścit trayoviṁśati-varṣāṇi jīviṣyanti anavarataṁ cātra kali-yuge kṣayam āyāty akhila evaiṣa janaḥ ||97||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **svīkaraṇameva vivāhahetuḥ, na tu smṛtyādyuktavidhiprakāraḥ | sadveśadhārī dāmbhikaḥ | kaliyuge kṣayamaśeṣaṁ yāti janaḥ kṣayamupaiṣyatītyanvayaḥ ||97||



**śrauta-smārta-dharme67 viplavam atyantam upagate kṣīṇa-prāye ca kalāv aśeṣa-jagat-sraṣṭuś carācara-guror ādi-madhyānta-rahitasya brahma-mayasyātma-rūpiṇo68 bhagavato vāsudevasyāṁśaḥ śambala-grāma-pradhāna-brāhmaṇasya viṣṇuyaśaso gṛhe’ṣṭa-guṇa-rddhi-samanvitaḥ kalki-rūpī jagaty atrāvatīryya sakala-mleccha-dasyu-duṣṭācaraṇa-cetasām aśeṣāṇām aparicchinna-śakti-māhātmyaḥ kṣayaṁ kariṣyati sva-dharmeṣu cākhilam eva69 saṁsthāpayiṣyati ||98|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **evaṁ kalerante kalkyavatāreṇa satyayugapravṛttimāha—śrautasmārta ity-ādinā ādimayasya sarvakāraṇarūpasyāntamayasya niṣedhāvadhibhūtasya ata eva sarvamayasya nikhilakāryamayasya | tato vikārādiprāptāvāha—brahmamayasya aṣṭaguṇārddhisamanvitaḥ | 



aṇimā laghimā prāptiḥ prākāmyaṁ vaśitā tathā | 

atra kāmāvasāyitvaṁ mahimeti guṇāṣṭakam || 



iti prokta-guṇayuktaḥ | anye tvanyathā guṇāṣṭakaṁ vadanti | 



aṇimā mahimā caiva laghimā garimā tathā | 

īśitvaṁ ca vaśitvaṁ ca prākāmyaṁ kāmameva ca iti ||98||



**anantaraṁ cāśeṣa-kaler avasāne vibuddhānām iva70 teṣām eva janapadānām amala-sphaṭika-viśuddha-matayo bhaviṣyanti ||99|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **prabuddhānāmityanena sattvaguṇodreko darśitaḥ | tena kālena kṛtānāmāhitaśaktīnāmutyarthaḥ ||99|| 



**teṣāṁ ca bīja-bhūtānām aśeṣa-manuṣyāṇāṁ pariṇatānām api tat-kāla-kṛtāpatya-prasūtir bhaviṣyati ||100|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : **tata kālakṛta iti pāṭhe prasūterviśeṣaṇam ||100|| 



**tāni ca tad-apatyāni kṛta-yugānusārīṇy eva bhaviṣyanti ||101||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kālasvabhāvādeva kṛtayugadharmānusārīṇi ||101|| 



**atrocyate—**

**yadā candraś ca sūryaś ca tathā tiṣyo bṛhaspatiḥ |**

**ekarāśau sameṣyanti tadā bhavati vai kṛtam ||102||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **etat sarvaṁ kasmin yoge bhaviṣyatītyapekṣāyāmāha | atrocyate iti | tiṣyaḥ puṣyaḥ, candrārkabṛhaspatīnāṁ tiṣyayoge kṛtaṁ satyayugaṁ bhaviṣyati | yadyapi iti dvādaśābdaṁ karkaṭasthe bṛhaspatī amāvāsyāyāṁ trayāṇaṁ puṣyarkṣeṇa yogaḥ syāt, tathāpyekarāśau sameṣyantīti sahapravesokternātiprasaṅgaḥ ||102||



**atītā vartamānāś ca tathaivānāgatāś ca ye |**

**ete vaṁśeṣu bhūpālāḥ kathitā muni-sattama ||103||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **uktaṁ rājavaṁśaṁ nigamayati atītaṁ iti | anāgatā bhūpālāśca uktāḥ ||103|| 



**yāvat parīkṣito janma yāvan nadnābhiṣecanam |**

**etad varṣa-sahasraṁ tu jñeyaṁ pañcāśad uttaram ||104||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **anāgataḥ kṣatriyavaṁśa kiyat kālaṁ sthāsyatītyapekṣāyāmāha—yāvad iti pañcadaśottarasahasravarṣaparyantaṁ śuddhaḥ kṣatriyavaṁśaḥ sthāsyati | anantaraṁ nandena sarvakṣatriyanāśād ity arthaḥ ||104||



**saptarṣīṇāṁ tu yau pūrvau dṛśyete hy uditau divi |**

**tayos tu madhye nakṣatraṁ dṛśyate yat samaṁ niśi ||105||**



**tena saptarṣayo yuktās tiṣṭhanty abda-śataṁ nṝṇām |**

**te tu pārīkṣite kāle maghāsv āsan dvijottama ||106||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kaleḥ pravṛtti vṛddhiṁ ca vaktuṁ tatkālalakṣaṇamāha—saptarṣīṇām iti | prāgagraṁ śakaṭākāraṁ tārāsaptakaṁ saptarṣimaṇḍala, tatra pūrvata īśākāre'gramadhyamūleṣu marīcisabhāryavaśiṣṭhāṅgirasaḥ, tataḥ paścime khaṭvākāre tārācatuṣke aiśānāgneya-nairṛta-vāyavya-koṇaṣvatri-pulastya-pulaha kratavo yathākramaṁ tatra yau pūrvau prathamoditau pulahaṛtusaṁjñau dṛśyate, tayostat pūrvayośca madhye samaṁ dakṣiṇottararekhāyāṁ samadeśāvasthitaṁ yadaśvinyādinakṣatreṣvanyatamanakṣatraṁ dṛśyete, tena tathaiva yuktā nṛṇāmabdaśataṁ tiṣṭhati ||106||



**tadā pravṛttaś ca kalir dvādaśābda-śatātmakaḥ ||107||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kālalakṣamuktvā kalipravṛttimāha—ta iti | tadā sandhyāsandhyāṁśābhyāṁ saha dvādaśābdaśatātmakaḥ kaliḥ pūrvasandhyā pūrvaṁ sandhyārūpeṇa pravṛtto'pi sandhyāḥ rūpamatikramya svena rūpeṇa pravṛtaḥ prakarṣeṇa vṛtta ity arthaḥ ||107|| 



**yadaiva bhagavān viṣṇor aṁśo yāto divaṁ dvija |**

**vasudeva-kulodbhūtas tadaivātrāgataḥ kaliḥ ||108||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **ete spaṣṭayati, yadaiveti dvābhyām ||108||



**yāvat sa pāda-padmābhyām pasparśemāṁ vasundharām |**

**tāvat pṛthvī-pariṣvaṅge samartho nābhavat kaliḥ ||109||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **pṛthvīpariṣvaṅge bhūmeḥ paribhave samartha ityukteḥ pūrvamapi kaliḥ praviṣṭa iti gamyate ||109|| 



**gate sanātanasyāṁśe viṣṇos tatra bhuvo divam |**

**tatyāja sānujo rājyaṁ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||110||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **sākṣāt kalipraveśe tu yudhiṣṭhirādibhiḥ svarājyaṁ parityaktamityāha—gata iti dvābhyām ||110||



**viparītāni dṛṣṭvā ca nimittāni hi pāṇḍavaḥ |**

**yāte kṛṣṇe cakārātha so’bhiṣekaṁ parīkṣitaḥ ||111||**



**prayāsyanti yadā caite pūrvāṣāḍhāṁ maharṣayaḥ |**

**tadā nandā prabhṛty eṣa gati-vṛddhiṁ gamiṣyati ||112||**



**yasmin kṛṣṇo divaṁ yātas tasminn eva tadāhani |**

**pratipannaṁ kali-yugaṁ tasya saṅkhyāṁ nibodha me ||113||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **pūrvoktameva kalipraveśakālamanūdya tata saṁkhyāmāha—yasminn ititribhiḥ ||113|| 



**trīṇi lakṣāṇi varṣāṇāṁ dvija mānuṣya-saṅkhyayā |**

**ṣaṣṭiś caiva sahasrāṇi bhaviṣyaty eṣa vai kaliḥ ||114||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **trīṇīti sandhyā-sandhyāṁśābhyāṁ vineti jñeyam ||114|| 



**śatāni tāni divyānāṁ sapta paṁ ca ca saṅkhyayā |**

**niḥśeṣeṇa gate tasmin bhaviṣyati punaḥ kṛtam ||115||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **divyāni divyasaṁkhyayā saṁkhyātāni saptapañcasaṁkhyayādvādaśābdaśatānītyarthaḥ | niḥśeṣeṇa tasmin gate satīti śeṣaḥ | kṛtaṁ kṛtayugam ||115||



**brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca dvija-sattama |**

**yuge yuge mahātmānaḥ samatītāḥ sahasraśaḥ ||116||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **brāhmaṇādivaṁśaḥ kṣatriyavaṁśaśca sakalaḥ kimiti naukta ityataḥ āha—brāhmaṇā iti dvābhyām ||116||



**bahutvān nāmadheyānāṁ parisaṅkhyā kule kule |**

**paunaruktyād dhi sāmyāc na mayā parikīrtitā ||117||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kule kule avāntarakuleṣu nāmadheyānāṁ parisaṁkhyā bahutvāt samānanāmatayā paunaruktyācca noktā ||117||



**devāpiḥ pauravo rājā puruś cekṣvāku-vaṁśajaḥ |**

**mahāyoga-balopetau kalāpa-grāma-saṁśritau ||118||**



**kṛte yuge tv ihāgamya kṣatra-pravartakau hi tau |**

**bhaviṣyato manor vaṁśa-bīja-bhūtau vyavasthitau ||119||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṣatrasya pravṛtakau bhaviṣyataḥ, yato manorvaṁśe somasūryavaṁśarūpa bījabhūtau vyavasthitau ||119|| 



**etena krama-yogena manu-putrair vasundharā |**

**kṛta-tretā-dvāparāṇi yugāni trīṇi bhujyate ||120||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kaleḥ sandhyāyāmeva kṣatriyasattvāt trīṇi yugāni bhujyata ityuktam ||120||



**kalau te bīja-bhūtā vai kecit tiṣṭhanti vai mune |  
yathaiva devāpi-purū sāmprataṁ samadhiṣṭhitau ||121||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **devāpi-maruvadanyatrāpi kalau brāhmaṇādīnāṁ bījabhūtānāṁ sthitimāha—kalau tviṭa iti ||121||



**eṣa tūddeśato vaṁśas tavokto bhūbhujāṁ mayā |**

**nikhilo gadituṁ śakyo naiṣa varṣa-śatair api ||122||**



**ete cānye ca bhūpālā yair atra kṣiti-maṇḍale |**

**kṛtaṁ mamatvaṁ mohāndhair nityaṁ heya-kalevare ||123||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **vaṁśakathanasya vairāgye tātparyamāha—ete ca iti | bhūmaṇḍale nitye kalpāntasthāyini tadapekṣayā anityāni asthirāṇi kalevarāṇi yeṣāṁ tathābhūtairapi mamatvaṁ kṛtam ||123|| 



**kathaṁ mameyaṁ acalā mat-putrasya kathaṁ mahī |**

**mad-vaṁśasyeti cintārtā jagmur antam ime nṛpāḥ ||124||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **mohāndhatvamevāha—kathaṁ mameyam iti dvābhyām ||124||



**tebhyaḥ pūrvatarāś cānye tebhyas tebhyas tathā pare |**

**bhaviṣyāś caiva yāsyanti teṣāṁ anye ca ye’py anu ||125||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tebhyastebhyaḥ pūrvatarā ityanenātītānāṁ mohāvasthā darśitā, evaṁ bhaviṣyā ityanāgatānāṁ mohāvasthā ||125||



**vilokyātmajayodyogaṁ yātrā-vyagrān narādhipān |**

**puṣpa-prahāsaiḥ śaradi hasantīva vasundharā ||126||**



**maitreya pṛthivī-gītān ślokāṁś cātra nibodha me |**

**yān āha dharma-dhvajine janakāyāsito muniḥ ||127||**



**pṛthivy uvāca—**

**katham eṣa narendrāṇāṁ moho buddhimatām api |**

**yena phena-sadharmāṇo’py ativiśvasta-cetasaḥ ||128||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **etadeva pṛthivīgītaiḥ prapañcayati—kathemeṣa iti navabhiḥ | phenasadharmāṇaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgurā ity arthaḥ ||128||



**pūrvam ātma-jayaṁ kṛtvā jetum icchanti mantriṇaḥ |**

**tato bhṛtyāṁś ca paurāṁś ca jigīṣante tathā ripūn ||129||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **pūrvamātmajayamiti ajitendriyāṇāṁ mantribhṛtyādijayābhāvāt ||129|| 



**krameṇānena jeṣyāmo vayaṁ pṛthvīṁ sa-sāgarām |**

**ity āsakta-dhiyo mṛtyuṁ na paśyanty avidūragam ||130||**



**samudrāvaraṇaṁ yāti bhū-maṇḍalam atho vaśam |**

**kiyad ātmajayasyaitan muktir ātma-jaye phalam ||131||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kiñcevaṁ sarvamātmavaśīkurvato mama bhuvo maṇḍalaṁ vaṁśa yāti | yadyapi tathāpyātmanāmindriyādīnāṁ jayāt jātametadanityaṁ rājyaṁ kiyadatyalpam | kṣayādātmajaye sati muktiratyantaṁ phalam ||131||  


**utsṛjya pūrvajā yātāyāṁ nādāya gataḥ pitā |**

**tāṁ mām atīva-mūḍhatvāj jetum icchanti pārthivāḥ ||132||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **anityatvamevāha—utsṛjya iti | pūrvajāḥ pūrveṣāmiti vā pāṭhaḥ ||132||



**mat-kṛte pitṛ-putrāṇāṁ bhrātṝṇāṁ cāpi vigrahaḥ |**

**jāyate’tyanta-mohena mamatvādṛta-cetasām ||133||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **rājye pitrādivairamapi doṣamāha—matkṛta iti ||133|| 



**pṛthvī mameyaṁ sakalā mamaiṣā **

**mad-anvayasyāpi ca śāśvatīyam |**

**yo yo mṛto hy atra babhūva rājā **

**kubuddhir āsīd iti tasya tasya ||134||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kiṁ ca mayi rājñāṁ mamatvabuddhirvṛthaivetyāha—pṛthvī mama iti | atra mayi yo yo rājā mṛto babhūva, tasya tasyaiveyaṁ kubuddhirāsīt, tataḥ pāramārthikaphalābhāvāt | anyatreti pāṭhe mṛtaḥ tvanyatra rājā babhūva, tasyāpi vāsanāvaśādiyameva kubuddhiḥ saṁsārapradāsīd ity arthaḥ ||134||



**dṛṣṭvā mamatvādṛta-cittam ekaṁ**

**vihāya māṁ mṛtyu-vaśaṁ vrajantam |**

**tasyānu yas tasya kathaṁ mamatvaṁ**

**hṛdyāspadaṁ mat-prasavaṁ karoti ||135||**



**pṛthvī mamaiṣāsu parityajaināṁ**

**vadanti ye dūtamukhaiḥ sva-śatrūn |**

**narādhipās teṣu mamātihāsaḥ**

**punaś ca mūḍheṣu dayābhyupaiti ||136||**



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**ity ete dharaṇī-gītāḥ ślokā maitreya yaiḥ śrutāḥ |**

**mamatvaṁ vilayaṁ yāti tapaty arke yathā himam ||137||**



**ity eṣa kathitaḥ samyaṅ manor vaṁśo mayā tava |**

**yatra sthiti-pravṛttasya viṣṇor aṁśāṁśakā nṛpāḥ ||138||71**



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe caturthe’ṁśe caturviṁśo’dhyāyaḥ ||





## dvitīya-bhāgaḥ

## pañcama-ṣaṣṭhāv aṁśau



viṣṇucitta-śrīdharasvāmināṁ vyākhyābhyāṁ saha |



There appears to be considerable variation in the Sridhar commentary. There is furthermore no chapter 6.9 in the Nag Publishers edition, where Vishnucitta's commentary comes to an end, though other editions with Sridhara do have that chapter with his commentary.
